// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).

{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

```dafny
// Count occurrences of value v in sequence s
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    assert 0 <= cnt8 <= |digits|; // added assertion
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
      assert cnt8 <= |digits|; // added assertion
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
    assert count == cnt8; // added assertion
    assert count <= n / 11; // added assertion
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
    assert count == n / 11; // added assertion
    assert count <= cnt8; // added assertion
  }
}
```

  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: i...

--- LLM RESPONSE (434 tokens, 9.73s) ---

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

{
  // Count occurrences of value v in sequence s
  ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
    decreases |s|
  {
    if |s| == 0 then 0
    else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
  }

  // Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
  // assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
  // assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
  // Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
  // (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
  ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
  {
    |assignment| == |digits| &&
    k >= 0 &&
    (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
    (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
      CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
      (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
  }

  // Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
  //   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
  //   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
  ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
  {
    k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
  }

  lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
    ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
    decreases |s|
  {
    if |s| > 0 {
      CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
    }
  }

  method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
    requires n == |digits|
    ensures Achievable(count, digits)
    ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
  {
    var cnt8 := 0;
    for i := 0 to |digits|
      invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    {
      if digits[i] == 8 {
        cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
      }
    }

    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
    if cnt8 < n / 11 {
      count := cnt8;
    } else {
      count := n / 11;
    }
    assert Achievable(count, digits);
    assert !Achievable(count + 1, digits);
  }
}

// Count occurrences of value v in sequence s
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

  }

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    invariant 0 <= cnt8 <= |digits|
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  assert CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8) > 0;
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
  assert Achievable(count, digits);
  assert !Achievable(count + 1, digits);
}

  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }

    }
  }

    count := n / 11;

{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  assert cnt8 >= 0; // non‑negativity of cnt8
  assert cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits, 8); // final count
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
  assert count <= n / 11; // bound on count
  assert 11 * count <= |digits|; // from bound on count
  assert count <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8); // from bound on count
  assert count >= 0; // non‑negativity of count
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  // Invariant: cnt8 equals the number of 8's in the prefix digits[..i]
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant 0 <= cnt8 <= |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
  assert Achievable(count, digits);
  assert !Achievable(count + 1, digits);
}

// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8

//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s

  }

// Count occurrences of value v in sequence s

{

}

// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    invariant 0 <= cnt8 <= |digits|
  {
    if i < |digits| && digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  assert CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
  assert Achievable(count, digits);
  assert !Achievable(count + 1, digits);
}

    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)

    assert 0 <= cnt8 <= i; // count of 8s cannot exceed processed length
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
      assert cnt8 <= i + 1; // after increment, still <= processed length
    }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);

    count := cnt8;

  assert count <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8); // from branching

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }
  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
  assert Achievable(count, digits);
  assert !Achievable(count + 1, digits);
}

    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

// Necessary and sufficient condition for forming k phone numbers from the cards:
//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s
ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

//   - Each phone number requires 11 cards  =>  11 * k <= |digits|
//   - Each phone number requires at least one 8  =>  k <= count of 8s

{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    invariant 0 <= cnt8 <= |digits|
  {
    if i < |digits| && digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
    invariant Achievable(cnt8, digits)
  {
    assert 0 <= i <= |digits|;
    assert cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8);
    if i < |digits| && digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
  assert Achievable(count, digits);
  assert !Achievable(count + 1, digits);
}

// Count occurrences of value v in sequence s
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

// Formalizes the problem statement: a valid assignment of cards to k phone numbers.
// assignment[i] == 0 means card i is unused.
// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and s...

--- LLM RESPONSE (434 tokens, 3.06s) ---
<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}

  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)

}

      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);

  } else {

  }

// assignment[i] == j (1 <= j <= k) means card i belongs to phone number j.
// Each phone number uses exactly 11 cards, at least one of which has digit 8
// (capturing: phone numbers have length 11 and start with 8).
ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{

  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&

// Count occurrences of value v in sequence s
ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost function CountOccurrences(s: seq<int>, v: int): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else (if s[|s|-1] == v then 1 else 0) + CountOccurrences(s[..|s|-1], v)
}

ghost predicate ValidPhoneAssignment(assignment: seq<int>, k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  |assignment| == |digits| &&
  k >= 0 &&
  (forall i | 0 <= i < |assignment| :: 0 <= assignment[i] <= k) &&
  (forall j | 1 <= j <= k ::
    CountOccurrences(assignment, j) == 11 &&
    (exists i | 0 <= i < |digits| :: assignment[i] == j && digits[i] == 8))
}

ghost predicate Achievable(k: int, digits: seq<int>)
{
  k >= 0 && 11 * k <= |digits| && k <= CountOccurrences(digits, 8)
}

lemma CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s: seq<int>, v: int)
  ensures CountOccurrences(s, v) >= 0
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| > 0 {
    CountOccurrencesNonNeg(s[..|s|-1], v);
  }
}

method PhoneNumbers(n: int, digits: seq<int>) returns (count: int)
  requires n == |digits|
  ensures Achievable(count, digits)
  ensures !Achievable(count + 1, digits)
{
  var cnt8 := 0;
  for i := 0 to |digits|
    invariant cnt8 == CountOccurrences(digits[..i], 8)
  {
    if digits[i] == 8 {
      cnt8 := cnt8 + 1;
    }
  }

  CountOccurrencesNonNeg(digits, 8);
  if cnt8 < n / 11 {
    count := cnt8;
  } else {
    count := n / 11;
  }
}
